<p><strong>Hostinger is one of the most budget-friendly web hosting providers, starting at just ‎<span class="pricing-link"><span data-currency="USD" class="currency-symbol ">$</span><span data-currency="USD" data-price="2.99" class="currency-value">2.99</span></span> per month.</strong> The catch? To secure the best deal, you have to commit to one of its years-long plans (up to four years), paid up front, ensuring a fixed discounted rate for the entire term. That’s a long commitment though – can Hostinger maintain its service quality over this period?</p>
<p>Our extensive and repeated testing suggests it most likely can. <strong>It specializes in shared WordPress hosting, targeting newcomers with ample support,</strong> making it ideal for personal sites, business landing pages, and small-to-medium online stores.</p>
<p>For traffic-heavy, resource-demanding websites, Hostinger offers VPS and cloud hosting, but these plans often lack value and flexibility when compared to higher-priced hosts.</p>
<p>Where Hostinger excels is as an entry-level shared web hosting solution, or for migrating from pricier providers. Most importantly, <strong>our tests have revealed that Hostinger offers shared hosting performance rivaling virtually all other budget hosts</strong> due to its LiteSpeed-based server infrastructure.</p>
<p>Notably, <strong>Hostinger&#8217;s website is available in numerous languages,</strong> with customer interfaces in Arabic, Chinese, French, German, Hindi, Indonesian, Lithuanian, Portuguese (including Brazilian Portuguese), Russian, Spanish (Argentina, Colombia, Mexico, and Spain), Turkish, and Ukrainian, catering to a global audience.</p>

<div class="section-content content">
<h3><div id="Features">A Highly-Optimized Platform With Plenty of Resources</div></h3>
<p>With prices being as low as they are, my anxious personality immediately identified two areas where Hostinger might be trying to pull one over on me: features and performance. Sure, I’d love to pay less than what the competitors charge, but I don’t want to get only some of what they provide.</p>
<p>Fortunately, I soon discovered that <strong>Hostinger provides a generous set of resources, plenty of built-in WordPress optimization, and all the critical features you need</strong> to get started. I focused my testing efforts on Hostinger’s WordPress Starter <span style="font-weight: 400;">(now Managed WordPress Premium)</span>. Here are the features that stood out to me.</p>
<h3>Optimized Performance From LiteSpeed Web Server</h3>
<figure class="wp-caption aligncenter"><span class="ll-img-wrapper "  style="padding:74.030354131535% 0 0; max-width: 850px;"><noscript><img src="https://dt2sdf0db8zob.cloudfront.net/wp-content/uploads/2024/04/file1-2.png"  width="1186" height="878" alt="Screenshot displaying Hostinger's site settings with LiteSpeed enabled." /></noscript><img data-src="https://dt2sdf0db8zob.cloudfront.net/wp-content/uploads/2024/04/file1-2.png"   width="1186" height="878" alt="Screenshot displaying Hostinger's site settings with LiteSpeed enabled." class=" ll-img"/></span><figcaption class="wp-caption-text"><em>New WordPress sites are pre-optimized for maximum speed with Hostinger</em></figcaption></figure>
<p><strong>Hostinger employs the impressively fast LiteSpeed web server</strong> – this is the software running on the physical server that delivers your website’s content to your visitors. LiteSpeed outperforms the more traditional Apache web server, upon which many other web hosts still rely due to its open-source (i.e. free) license.</p>
<p>LiteSpeed itself already offers great performance, but <strong>its LiteSpeed Cache for WordPress plugin stores pre-loaded (cached) copies of your web pages</strong>, which can then be more quickly delivered to your visitors.</p>
<div class="shortcode-external-button-link"><a href="https://www.websiteplanet.com/goto.php?id=46365&lang=en&deep_id=877905&deep_name=Wordpress hosting&btn_name=ButtonExternalUrl_46365_vendor_46365_852709&post_id=46365&pageview_id=0&direct_link=&type=vendor&amp=0" data-id="46365" rel="sponsored noopener norefferer" class="clickoutLink shortC" target="_blank" onclick="trackClickout('event', 'clickout', 'ButtonExternalUrl_46365_vendor_46365_852709', 'hostinger', this,  true, ReturnPopup  );">Discover More Hostinger Features &gt;&gt;</a></div>
<h3>Generous With Bandwidth, SSD Storage, and Number of Sites</h3>
<p>With such affordable prices, I expected Hostinger to be tight on resources. Many budget web hosts cut costs by allocating fewer resources per customer, because this allows them to jam more hosting accounts onto each server.</p>
<p>But Hostinger offers plenty of resources for its low rates – <strong>the cheapest WordPress plan includes support for 100 websites, 100 GB of SSD storage, and unlimited bandwidth</strong>. This is more than what many other budget hosts offer with their most expensive plans. You’ll have plenty of room to grow and develop your online presence, and you’ll be able to host many sites at once.</p>
<h3>Automatic Backups With One-Click Restoration</h3>
<figure class="wp-caption aligncenter"><span class="ll-img-wrapper "  style="padding:57.963446475196% 0 0; max-width: 850px;"><noscript><img src="https://dt2sdf0db8zob.cloudfront.net/wp-content/uploads/2024/04/file1-3.png"  width="1532" height="888" alt="Screenshot of Hostinger's backup management page" /></noscript><img data-src="https://dt2sdf0db8zob.cloudfront.net/wp-content/uploads/2024/04/file1-3.png"   width="1532" height="888" alt="Screenshot of Hostinger's backup management page" class=" ll-img"/></span><figcaption class="wp-caption-text"><em>Hostinger gives you plenty of control over your backups</em></figcaption></figure>
<p>Data loss can be absolutely ruinous for an online business. You don’t want to spend hours working on your site just to lose it all to a wifi glitch, or even to an honest mistake. Thankfully, <strong>Hostinger offers a flexible backup tool that allows you to create, download, or restore backups</strong>.</p>
<p>In addition, <strong>Hostinger offers weekly automatic backups – as it does with the WordPress Starter <b>(now Managed WordPress Premium)</b> plan – with a free upgrade to daily automatic backups with higher-tier shared plans</strong>. Alternatively, you can pay for this feature as an add-on.</p>
<h3>Unlimited Free SSL and a Robust Security Suite</h3>
<p>No matter how tight your budget is, you can’t afford to go with a web host that’ll leave your site vulnerable to malware or DDoS attacks. Fortunately, Hostinger understands the importance of security and provides protection from an array of potential online threats.</p>
<p><strong>Every plan includes free SSL for all your sites, an in-house-developed web application firewall, an automatic malware scanner, and Cloudflare DDoS protection for Hostinger’s nameservers</strong> – this is not to be confused with Cloudflare’s content delivery network (CDN), which isn’t enabled by default. This may not be the most advanced security suite out there – but it’ll keep you safe from the most common threats. It’s also more than what you’d get with most other budget hosts.</p>

<h2 class="section-title section-title-ease-of-use"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" viewBox="0 0 30 30" aria-label="ease-of-use" role="img"><path d="m7.8,29l-6.8,0c-0.6,0 -1,-0.4 -1,-1l0,-16.7c0,-0.6 0.4,-1 1,-1l6.8,0c0.6,0 1,0.4 1,1l0,16.7c0,0.5 -0.5,1 -1,1zm-5.8,-2l4.8,0l0,-14.7l-4.8,0l0,14.7z"/><path d="m19.2,29l-5.7,0c-1.9,0 -3.9,-0.6 -5.4,-1.8l-1,-0.7c-0.3,-0.2 -0.4,-0.5 -0.4,-0.8l0,-14.3c0,-0.2 0,-0.3 0.1,-0.5l4.6,-8.2c0.4,-0.7 1.1,-1.3 1.9,-1.6c0.8,-0.2 1.7,-0.1 2.5,0.3c1,0.6 1.6,1.7 1.5,2.9l-0.5,6l8.8,0c1.4,0 2.6,0.6 3.4,1.7s1.1,2.5 0.7,3.8c-0.5,1.5 -3.1,8.8 -4.2,10.1c-1.4,2 -3.8,3.1 -6.3,3.1zm-10.4,-3.9l0.6,0.4c1.2,0.9 2.7,1.4 4.2,1.4l5.7,0c1.9,0 3.7,-0.8 4.8,-2.3c0.6,-0.8 2.6,-6 3.8,-9.5c0.2,-0.7 0.1,-1.4 -0.4,-2c-0.4,-0.6 -1.1,-0.9 -1.8,-0.9l-9.9,0c-0.3,0 -0.5,-0.1 -0.7,-0.3s-0.3,-0.5 -0.3,-0.8l0.5,-7c0,-0.4 -0.2,-0.8 -0.5,-1c-0.3,-0.2 -0.6,-0.2 -0.9,-0.1c-0.3,0.1 -0.5,0.3 -0.7,0.6l-4.5,8l0,13.5l0.1,0z"/></svg><span id="ease-of-use">Ease of use</span></h2>

<div class="section-content content">
<h3>Hostinger Automates Setup To Get You Started</h3>
<p>Overall, <strong>Hostinger offers a remarkably easy platform to work with, from sign-up to developing and managing your website</strong>. We had no trouble purchasing a plan and building our test website.</p>
<p><strong>This is due in part to Hostinger’s proprietary control panel, hPanel, which is really easy to navigate (more on this later)</strong>. Here’s what you can expect when you sign up for an account, and set up a site on Hostinger’s platform.</p>
<h3>Creating a New Account</h3>
<p>Signing up with Hostinger was refreshingly easy. Hosting plans were clearly laid out, and we had no problems discerning what was included with each of them. The WordPress Starter (now Managed WordPress Premium) plan offers a free domain name <strong>if you choose an annual or longer billing cycle</strong>, which was a nice addition. This is the case with every WordPress plan.</p>
<p><strong>What’s particularly nice is that we only had to provide a minimum of information</strong> – there was no huge, time-consuming form requiring a ridiculous amount of personal data. We were also given the option to sign-up with a Facebook or Google account to simplify the process.</p>
<p>Accepted payment methods include all major credit cards, PayPal, Google Pay, AliPay, and even some cryptocurrencies like Bitcoin. Thankfully, <strong>Hostinger didn’t pre-select any add-ons or try to upsell us during checkout</strong>. It was always clear how much we were paying, and for what services.</p>
<p>After payment was complete, our account was set up. <strong>We were ready to connect our domain and install WordPress in under a minute</strong>.</p>
<h3>Connecting a Domain and Installing WordPress</h3>
<p>Once your account has been created, Hostinger takes you through some set-up steps.<strong> We were first presented with a short questionnaire, the purpose of which was to <b>set up the hosting environment and to</b> auto-configure LiteSpeed’s caching</strong> to maximize performance based on your particular needs. This allows you to take full advantage of LiteSpeed without having to figure how to optimize the settings yourself.</p>
<p>From there,<strong> we were asked if we would like to install WordPress automatically</strong>. This again was really quick and easy, as I only had to enter an administrator email address and password, and optionally choose a starter theme.</p>
<figure class="wp-caption aligncenter"><span class="ll-img-wrapper "  style="padding:53.074027603513% 0 0; max-width: 850px;"><noscript><img src="https://dt2sdf0db8zob.cloudfront.net/wp-content/uploads/2024/04/file1-4.png"  width="1594" height="846" alt="Screenshot of Hostinger's WordPress auto-installation setup screen" /></noscript><img data-src="https://dt2sdf0db8zob.cloudfront.net/wp-content/uploads/2024/04/file1-4.png"   width="1594" height="846" alt="Screenshot of Hostinger's WordPress auto-installation setup screen" class=" ll-img"/></span><figcaption class="wp-caption-text"><em>Hostinger can optionally install the WooCommerce plugin with WordPress</em></figcaption></figure>
<p>With that, the next step was connecting a domain name. As we had signed up for the WordPress Premium plan on an annual billing cycle, <strong>we were able to claim a free domain name</strong>. Be aware that not all domain extensions are available with Hostinger’s free domain name offer, though the popular .com is included.</p>
<p>After choosing a domain name and extension, we just had to pick a data center. We went with a US-based location, but you should choose the location nearest to your target audience. Once this was done, we were given a summary of the information we had entered, which we confirmed to begin installing WordPress and registering our domain name.</p>
<p>Five minutes later, WordPress installation and domain registration were complete. <strong>Our domain was automatically connected to our site as part of the setup process</strong>, but we had to wait some hours for DNS (domain name system) propagation to complete. This is an unavoidable process that takes place whenever you connect a new domain, and it may prevent your WordPress installation from being accessible online until it is complete.</p>
<p><strong>After an hour or two of waiting, DNS propagation was complete</strong>. We were then able to upload our custom WordPress theme and access our test website online. Overall, Hostinger sets up nearly all of the hosting and basic WordPress framework for you.</p>
<h3>Beginner-Friendly hPanel Makes Hosting Easy To Manage</h3>
<p><strong>Hostinger has developed its own proprietary control panel, called hPanel</strong>. It’s a joy to use – it’s easy to navigate, cleanly designed, and gives you access to all the basic processes you need to manage your sites.</p>
<p>That said, it can be a bit slow at times, depending on which settings you’re accessing. Entering the File Manager can take several seconds of loading, for example. Accessing the WordPress Admin area can also take several seconds – though the fact that the WordPress login process is reduced to a single click in hPanel makes up for the loading time.</p>
<h3>Flexible Drag-and-Drop Site Builder, Included Free</h3>
<figure class="wp-caption aligncenter"><span class="ll-img-wrapper "  style="padding:64.022662889518% 0 0; max-width: 850px;"><noscript><img src="https://dt2sdf0db8zob.cloudfront.net/wp-content/uploads/2024/04/file1-5.png"  width="1412" height="904" alt="Screenshot of Hostinger's AI builder" /></noscript><img data-src="https://dt2sdf0db8zob.cloudfront.net/wp-content/uploads/2024/04/file1-5.png"   width="1412" height="904" alt="Screenshot of Hostinger's AI builder" class=" ll-img"/></span><figcaption class="wp-caption-text"><em>Hostinger’s AI website builder is the latest addition to its list of hosting features</em></figcaption></figure>
<p>If you want to design a website quickly and easily without having to learn WordPress, <strong>Hostinger includes a free AI site builder with its hosting plans</strong>. Like hPanel, this has also been developed in-house by Hostinger, and it allows you to build websites via a drag-and-drop interface.</p>
<p>Even if you already have a WordPress-based website, <strong>you can try switching over to the builder app for a limited time</strong>, and if you don’t like it, your original site will be restored, free of charge.</p>
<h3>One-Click Installer for 100+ Apps</h3>
<p>In addition to a simple installation for WordPress, <strong>Hostinger’s Auto Installer lets you easily install over 100+ applications</strong>. This includes alternative CMSs (content management systems) like Joomla or Drupal, along with apps for database management, message boards, and more.</p>
<p>The selection may not seem to be quite as extensive as some other auto installers, but it offers all of the most useful and popular apps.</p>
</div>
</section>

<h2 class="section-title section-title-perfomance"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" viewBox="0 0 512 512" aria-label="perfomance" role="img"><path d="m437.00002,113c-48.4,-48.4 -112.6,-75 -181,-75s-132.7,26.6 -181,75c-48.4,48.4 -75,112.6 -75,181c0,65.4 24.7,127.6 69.4,175.3l4.4,4.7l364.3,0l4.4,-4.7c44.8,-47.6 69.4,-109.9 69.4,-175.3c0.1,-68.4 -26.5,-132.7 -74.9,-181l0,0zm-12,331l-338,0c-6.8,-7.7 -13.1,-15.8 -18.8,-24.3l33.4,-19.3l-15,-26l-33.4,19.3c-13,-26.3 -20.7,-55.1 -22.7,-84.8l38.5,0l0,-30l-38.5,0c2,-30.2 10,-58.9 22.7,-84.7l33.3,19.2l15,-26l-33.3,-19.2c16.4,-24.5 37.5,-45.6 62,-62l19.2,33.3l26,-15l-19.2,-33.3c25.9,-12.8 54.5,-20.7 84.7,-22.7l0,38.5l30,0l0,-38.5c30.2,2 58.9,10 84.7,22.7l-19.2,33.3l26,15l19.2,-33.3c24.5,16.4 45.6,37.5 62,62l-33.3,19.2l15,26l33.3,-19.2c12.8,25.9 20.7,54.5 22.7,84.7l-38.3,0l0,30l38.5,0c-2,29.7 -9.7,58.5 -22.7,84.8l-33.4,-19.3l-15,26l33.4,19.3c-5.7,8.5 -11.9,16.6 -18.8,24.3l0,0z"/><path d="m272.20002,290.3l0,-94l-30,0l0,94c-19.8,6.4 -34.3,25 -34.3,46.9c0,27.2 22.1,49.3 49.3,49.3s49.3,-22.1 49.3,-49.3c0,-21.9 -14.5,-40.5 -34.3,-46.9zm-15,66.2c-10.6,0 -19.3,-8.6 -19.3,-19.3s8.6,-19.3 19.3,-19.3c10.6,0 19.3,8.6 19.3,19.3s-8.7,19.3 -19.3,19.3z"/></svg><span id="perfomance">Performance</span></h2>
</div>
<div class="section-content content">
<h3><div id="Performance">One of the Fastest Budget Web Hosts Out There</div></h3>
<p>Despite being significantly cheaper than many popular entry-level hosts, <strong>Hostinger excelled in our performance tests</strong>. It was easily one of the best-performing shared hosting providers we’ve ever tested, and it wasn’t too far behind some of the top premium hosting providers.</p>
<p>Hostinger provides data centers located in the US, Europe, Asia, and South America. If your website is aimed at attracting visitors from Africa, Australia, or the Middle East, it&#8217;s advisable to select the closest accessible data center to their respective locations.</p>
<p>To test Hostinger fairly, <strong>we built a website to simulate an average promotional site, filled with text, high-quality images, custom fonts, and plenty of complex code for interactive elements</strong>. We then put this website through multiple third-party testing tools – namely GTmetrix, Sucuri Load Time Tester, and UptimeRobot.</p>
<figure id="attachment_3307874" aria-describedby="caption-attachment-3307874"class="wp-caption aligncenter"><span class="ll-img-wrapper "  style="padding:62.154696132597% 0 0; max-width: 850px;"><noscript><img src="https://dt2sdf0db8zob.cloudfront.net/wp-content/uploads/2018/03/OPT-2024-Hostinger-Review-__IMAGES__-06-e1714405345889.png"  width="1810" height="1125" alt="Nutritionistica WordPress test website" /></noscript><img data-src="https://dt2sdf0db8zob.cloudfront.net/wp-content/uploads/2018/03/OPT-2024-Hostinger-Review-__IMAGES__-06-e1714405345889.png"   width="1810" height="1125" alt="Nutritionistica WordPress test website" class="wp-image-3307874 size-full ll-img"/></span><figcaption id="caption-attachment-3307874"class="wp-caption-text">Our custom test site has all the typical elements of an e-commerce site</figcaption></figure>
<div class="hightlight-paragraph hightlight-paragraph-transparent">Our test site with Hostinger achieved a typical loading time of about 0.8s and 100% uptime over a month. Put simply, it would be difficult to find better performance than this at Hostinger’s prices – see the impressive results for yourself below.</div>
<h3>GTmetrix</h3>
<p><strong>We used GTmetrix to test our website’s performance in a local setting</strong>. To do this, we selected a source server in the US, not too far away from our test site’s data center. We then completed a week-long performance analysis with hourly speed tests.</p>
<figure class="wp-caption aligncenter"><span class="ll-img-wrapper "  style="padding:59.021406727829% 0 0; max-width: 850px;"><noscript><img src="https://dt2sdf0db8zob.cloudfront.net/wp-content/uploads/2024/04/file1-6.png"  width="1308" height="772" alt="Screenshot of a GTmetrix test performed on a site hosted by Hostinger" /></noscript><img data-src="https://dt2sdf0db8zob.cloudfront.net/wp-content/uploads/2024/04/file1-6.png"   width="1308" height="772" alt="Screenshot of a GTmetrix test performed on a site hosted by Hostinger" class=" ll-img"/></span><figcaption class="wp-caption-text"><em>GTmetrix gave Hostinger an A rating</em></figcaption></figure>
<p>So, what did we find? <strong>During a week of testing, our website on Hostinger’s server achieved a typical Fully Loaded Time of just 0.8s</strong>. To put that in perspective, most other budget hosts hover around 2s to 3s – Hostinger manages to be several times faster.</p>
<p>How does it do this? Well, it is due in part to the default LiteSpeed optimization settings enabled by Hostinger when we first installed WordPress. For example,<strong> the default image compression reduced the total content on our test page in size from about 1 MB to just under 800 KB</strong>, allowing the page to load more quickly.</p>
<figure class="wp-caption aligncenter"><span class="ll-img-wrapper "  style="padding:44.192634560907% 0 0; max-width: 850px;"><noscript><img src="https://dt2sdf0db8zob.cloudfront.net/wp-content/uploads/2024/04/file1-7.png"  width="1412" height="624" alt="GTmetrix graph showing Hostinger's performance over a week" /></noscript><img data-src="https://dt2sdf0db8zob.cloudfront.net/wp-content/uploads/2024/04/file1-7.png"   width="1412" height="624" alt="GTmetrix graph showing Hostinger's performance over a week" class=" ll-img"/></span><figcaption class="wp-caption-text"><em>Besides a few hiccups, Hostinger’s performance was consistent</em></figcaption></figure>
<p>There were a few instances where our site took 1.5s to 2.0s to load. However, even these worst-case results are still within acceptable guidelines for visitor retention. And notably, as each of our tests is conducted from a “fresh” browser instance, some of the cache settings don’t affect these results – but<strong> a real website visitor should see the page load even faster on repeat visits</strong>.</p>
<p><strong>The results for Time to First Byte – the amount of time it takes for the server to start sending website data – were typically around 0.2s</strong>. This is a very good speed – it isn’t unusual to see this number at 0.5s or higher from shared hosting services.</p>
<h3>Sucuri Load Time Tester</h3>
<p>Next, we wanted to take a look at how Hostinger performed on a global scale. To do this, we used Sucuri’s Load Time Tester.</p>
<div class="hightlight-paragraph hightlight-paragraph-transparent">To get the best loading speeds on an international scale, you’ll usually need to have a CDN (content delivery network) active. This saves copies of your website’s content (images and code, for example) on servers around the world, so visitors far away from your chosen data center can access some of your content from a server that is closer to them. Most providers do not have a CDN pre-enabled, requiring you to set one up yourself.</div>
<p>While Hostinger supports Cloudflare’s CDN, you’ll have to sign up for an account and configure it yourself, even if you’re just using the free Cloudflare plan. As this isn’t a straightforward process, we don’t enable it – <strong>we test hosting plans “out of the box” in their default state, so we can tell you how well they will work for beginner users</strong>.</p>
<figure class="wp-caption aligncenter"><span class="ll-img-wrapper "  style="padding:50.42492917847% 0 0; max-width: 850px;"><noscript><img src="https://dt2sdf0db8zob.cloudfront.net/wp-content/uploads/2024/04/file1-8.png"  width="1412" height="712" alt="Hostinger performance test results from Sucuri Load Time Tester" /></noscript><img data-src="https://dt2sdf0db8zob.cloudfront.net/wp-content/uploads/2024/04/file1-8.png"   width="1412" height="712" alt="Hostinger performance test results from Sucuri Load Time Tester" class=" ll-img"/></span><figcaption class="wp-caption-text"><em>With a CDN, Hostinger would perform better globally, but these results are pretty good</em></figcaption></figure>
<p>The results were surprising. <strong>Our test site achieved loading speeds of about 1s in Europe and South America, despite being hosted at one of Hostinger’s US data centers</strong>.</p>
<p>While it was far slower in Singapore and Australia, reaching around 2s, this is still well within acceptable limits. In fact, these results are better than some of the budget hosts in these regions can deliver on their own home turf.</p>
<h3>UptimeRobot</h3>
<p>Finally, we measured Hostinger’s reliability. After all, it doesn’t matter how fast a host can make your website load if it’s rarely online to begin with.</p>
<p><strong>To test Hostinger’s uptime, we monitored our test website with UptimeRobot for an entire month</strong>. Whenever an instance of downtime occurred, it would be recorded.</p>
<figure class="wp-caption aligncenter"><span class="ll-img-wrapper "  style="padding:40.509915014164% 0 0; max-width: 850px;"><noscript><img src="https://dt2sdf0db8zob.cloudfront.net/wp-content/uploads/2024/04/file1-9.png"  width="1412" height="572" alt="Screenshot of an UptimeRobot test for Hostinger" /></noscript><img data-src="https://dt2sdf0db8zob.cloudfront.net/wp-content/uploads/2024/04/file1-9.png"   width="1412" height="572" alt="Screenshot of an UptimeRobot test for Hostinger" class=" ll-img"/></span><figcaption class="wp-caption-text"><em>It really doesn’t get better than this – well done, Hostinger</em></figcaption></figure>
<p><strong>Amazingly, there were <em>no</em> instances of downtime to record</strong>. Our test site was online and available for the duration of the testing period. Hosting providers with much more expensive plans sometimes struggle to match this result.</p>
<p><strong>Hostinger also offers a 99.9% uptime guarantee</strong>. If Hostinger fails to achieve this uptime within a specific month, you can request compensation in the form of service credits. This is not unique since a 99.9% uptime guarantee is the industry standard.</p>
<p><strong>Hostinger is a bit stingy with credits if you are entitled to compensation</strong>. You’d only be due 5% credit towards your next monthly bill. Thankfully, by our tests, it doesn’t look like you’ll frequently need to claim compensation, if ever.</p>
</div>
</section>

<div class="section-rating rating"><span class="wsp-star-block star-rating-90 vendor-medium"></span><span class="stars-score">4.4</span></div>
<h2 class="section-title section-title-support"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" viewBox="0 0 28 28" aria-label="support" role="img"><path d="m14,28.00001c-7.7,0 -14,-6.3 -14,-14s6.3,-14 14,-14s14,6.3 14,14s-6.3,14 -14,14zm0,-26c-6.6,0 -12,5.4 -12,12s5.4,12 12,12s12,-5.4 12,-12s-5.4,-12 -12,-12zm0,20.8c-4.9,0 -8.8,-3.9 -8.8,-8.8s3.9,-8.8 8.8,-8.8s8.8,3.9 8.8,8.8s-3.9,8.8 -8.8,8.8zm0,-15.6c-3.7,0 -6.8,3.1 -6.8,6.8s3.1,6.8 6.8,6.8s6.8,-3.1 6.8,-6.8s-3.1,-6.8 -6.8,-6.8z"/><path d="m19.5,9.50001c-0.3,0 -0.5,-0.1 -0.7,-0.3c-0.4,-0.4 -0.4,-1 0,-1.4l3.7,-3.7c0.4,-0.4 1,-0.4 1.4,0s0.4,1 0,1.4l-3.7,3.7c-0.2,0.2 -0.4,0.3 -0.7,0.3z"/><path d="m4.8,24.20001c-0.3,0 -0.5,-0.1 -0.7,-0.3c-0.4,-0.4 -0.4,-1 0,-1.4l3.7,-3.7c0.4,-0.4 1,-0.4 1.4,0s0.4,1 0,1.4l-3.7,3.7c-0.2,0.2 -0.4,0.3 -0.7,0.3z"/><path d="m23.2,24.20001c-0.3,0 -0.5,-0.1 -0.7,-0.3l-3.7,-3.7c-0.4,-0.4 -0.4,-1 0,-1.4s1,-0.4 1.4,0l3.7,3.7c0.4,0.4 0.4,1 0,1.4c-0.2,0.2 -0.5,0.3 -0.7,0.3z"/><path d="m8.5,9.50001c-0.3,0 -0.5,-0.1 -0.7,-0.3l-3.7,-3.7c-0.4,-0.4 -0.4,-1 0,-1.4s1,-0.4 1.4,0l3.7,3.7c0.4,0.4 0.4,1 0,1.4c-0.2,0.2 -0.5,0.3 -0.7,0.3z"/></svg><span id="support">Support</span></h2>
</div>
<div class="section-content content">
<h3><div id="Support"><div id="support2"></div>Polite but Primarily Relies on Links to Documentation</div></h3>
<p><strong>Hostinger’s support service is available 24/7 through live chat and email</strong>. While budget hosts often say they provide 24/7 technical support, you might have to wait a long time for an agent to become available.</p>
<p>The quality of the support itself may vary as well – <strong>some hosts save money by outsourcing support to third-party support teams who don’t have an understanding of hosting in general</strong>, never mind your particular issue.</p>
<p>So, does Hostinger have these problems? To find out, I pretended to be a complete newbie to web hosting, and asked some basic questions.</p>
<p><strong>You can easily contact Hostinger support from anywhere in hPanel by clicking the speech bubble icon</strong> on the bottom right of the dashboard. This will take you to the support screen, where you will first be required to select a topic relevant to your issue. When you click one of these, Hostinger will display links to knowledge base documentation on your chosen topic.</p>
<p>For basic queries, this can be really useful, as you’ll likely find the answer to your question in one of these articles. <strong>Hostinger’s knowledge base is fairly extensive, and filled with concise step-by-step guides for all the basics</strong> – some tutorials even include video guides.</p>
<p>If none of the suggested articles turn out to be of any help, you are then given the option to contact support. I did so via live chat, hoping to get a quick response.</p>
<figure class="wp-caption aligncenter"><span class="ll-img-wrapper "  style="padding:67.868338557994% 0 0; max-width: 850px;"><noscript><img src="https://dt2sdf0db8zob.cloudfront.net/wp-content/uploads/2024/04/file1-10.png"  width="1276" height="866" alt="Screenshot of a Hostinger live chat support interaction" /></noscript><img data-src="https://dt2sdf0db8zob.cloudfront.net/wp-content/uploads/2024/04/file1-10.png"   width="1276" height="866" alt="Screenshot of a Hostinger live chat support interaction" class=" ll-img"/></span><figcaption class="wp-caption-text"><em>Hostinger’s support agent was polite and friendly</em></figcaption></figure>
<p><strong>I was met with a banner stating that live chat agents typically respond in under 10 minutes</strong> – a perfectly mediocre response time. I typed out a question asking how I could optimize my site for faster performance, and waited.</p>
<p><strong>14 minutes later, I got my response</strong>. The Hostinger support agent was friendly and quick to respond to subsequent queries. <strong>They answered all my questions with links to the knowledge base</strong>, even when I tried to ask for more direct recommendations for WordPress optimization plugins.</p>
<p>This was just OK. The linked articles provided helpful, relevant information, but I wanted more personalized help. The support agent never asked about my website specifics or current loading speed, not even once. Call me cynical, but if your live support agents can only share documentation links, they might as well be bots.</p>
<p><strong>Next up, I tried email support</strong>. I asked how to set up a CDN to speed up my website. Hostinger’s email support only promises a reply within a single business day, so I prepared myself for a longer wait.</p>
<p>Surprisingly, after just a couple of minutes, I got a response from an agent stating they were looking into my query. Then, <strong>22 minutes after my initial email, I got a detailed response to my question, which is pretty fast for email support</strong>. It wasn’t too far behind the wait time for live chat.</p>
<figure class="wp-caption aligncenter"><span class="ll-img-wrapper "  style="padding:63.663220088626% 0 0; max-width: 850px;"><noscript><img src="https://dt2sdf0db8zob.cloudfront.net/wp-content/uploads/2024/04/file1-11.png"  width="1354" height="862" alt="Screenshot of a Hostinger email support interaction" /></noscript><img data-src="https://dt2sdf0db8zob.cloudfront.net/wp-content/uploads/2024/04/file1-11.png"   width="1354" height="862" alt="Screenshot of a Hostinger email support interaction" class=" ll-img"/></span><figcaption class="wp-caption-text"><em>It seems Hostinger’s support agents really know what they&#8217;re talking about</em></figcaption></figure>
<p>This was a similar level of quality to my previous live chat experience. <strong>They sent me links to guides on configuring a CDN, which gave me everything I needed to know</strong>. They also sent me some extra resources on site performance optimization, which was a nice touch that I was grateful for.</p>
<p>Overall, Hostinger’s support is a little slow, but helpful. That said,<strong> the support agents seem reluctant to go the extra mile, or to provide detailed help with queries</strong> that are too complex to be answered by a short knowledge base article.</p>
<p>Still, compared to the terrible experiences I’ve had with some other hosting support services, support quality was pretty decent overall.</p>
</div>
</section>

<h2 class="section-title section-title-pricing"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" viewBox="0 0 32 32" aria-label="pricing" role="img"><path </div>
<div class="section-content content">
<h3><div id="Pricing2"><div id="Pricing"></div>Massive Discounts for New Customers (and a Free Domain Name With Certain Plans)</div></h3>
<p>Pricing is usually what draws customers to Hostinger in the first place. <strong>Hostinger is easily one of the most affordable options for shared and WordPress hosting, with prices starting as low as</strong> <strong><span class="pricing-link"><span data-currency="USD" class="currency-symbol ">$</span><span data-currency="USD" data-price="2.99" class="currency-value">2.99</span></span></strong> <strong>per month</strong>. These can be purchased on monthly, annual, biennial, and quadrennial (that’s 4 years!) billing cycles.</p>
<p>Signing up for four years gets you the best prices, but it also locks you into the longest commitment. The monthly plans are rather poor value, though you can still get a good deal with the annual or biennial plans. <strong>Hostinger offers a risk-free 30-day money-back guarantee</strong>, so if you aren’t satisfied, you can cancel within the first month for a full refund.</p>

<p></p> <strong> 
<h3 class="shortcode-faq-question-inline">What is Hostinger best used for?</h3>
<p></p> </strong><span class="shortcode-faq-answer-inline">It depends on your needs. We don’t recommend Hostinger’s shared services for an e-commerce site that gets an enormous volume of traffic or a custom-built web application that needs a really flexible hosting environment. 
<p></p> However, Hostinger is one of your best options for a beginner-friendly service to host a basic website. It’s very affordable and offers some of <a href="#Performance" onclick="trackClickout('event', 'clickin', 'anchorLink', 'performance', this,  );">the fastest performance we’ve seen from a shared host</a>.</span><strong> 
<h3 class="shortcode-faq-question-inline">What are the cons of Hostinger?</h3>
<p></p> </strong><span class="shortcode-faq-answer-inline">Hostinger is primarily known as a shared hosting provider. While it does offer premium solutions such as VPS and cloud hosting, these aren’t its specialty – and these plans tend to lack value when compared with competing solutions from other providers. Also, <a href="#Support" onclick="trackClickout('event', 'clickin', 'anchorLink', 'support', this,  );">the 24/7 support may take a while to respond, and it failed to go the extra mile in our tests</a>.</span><strong> 
<h3 class="shortcode-faq-question-inline">What makes Hostinger hosting plans worth considering?</h3>
<p></p> </strong><span class="shortcode-faq-answer-inline">Hostinger actually topped our list of the best web hosting providers for 2024. This is primarily because <a href="#Features" onclick="trackClickout('event', 'clickin', 'anchorLink', 'features', this,  );">it combines superb performance and generous plan packages</a> with low prices. That said, it isn’t the perfect fit for everyone. I’d recommend taking a look at the other hosting providers on our list if Hostinger doesn’t seem right for you.</span><strong> 
<h3 class="shortcode-faq-question-inline">Does Hostinger cost more when you renew?</h3>
<p></p> </strong><span class="shortcode-faq-answer-inline">Yes. <a href="#Pricing2" onclick="trackClickout('event', 'clickin', 'anchorLink', 'pricing2', this,  );">When the discounts on your initial hosting term end</a>, Hostinger renews at the full price. This can mean quite a steep increase, so be wary when you sign up. That said, Hostinger is still fairly affordable even after renewal when compared to the long-term pricing of other budget hosts.</span> 
    </div>

                                        <div class="review-title">Dhocking communications.</div>                    <p class="review-text">After signing up I tried to start the migration process for a WordPress site built using the Divi builder. Divi is crucial to me as I’ve paid for a lifetime license and I like it. I tried searching on the subject and found endless articles on WP but no mention of Divi. I tried to open a chat but the window was unintuitive despite my 25 years of being a hosting customer with multiple suppliers. Sending an email to support@... I got replies directing me to knowledgebase articles but ignoring my question. The screen shots didn’t match what I saw on the screen. Even in those emails no mention of Divi. Even trying to find the chat window or ask the question the next day I couldn’t find the chat window, the floating icon is there (sometimes) but even then it still seemed to send me to the knowledgebase. This is all despite their basic stating that it’s suitable for hobbyists. Eventually, I managed to initiate a chat but only when I was asking for a refund. 

It’s a great value service but if you are not doing this every day or you have to do a new process occasionally expect to be left high and dry. It’s almost as though this is a company that doesn’t want to communicate with its customers.</p>
